# Changelog

Alle wichtigen Г„nderungen an diesem Projekt werden in dieser Datei dokumentiert.

Das Format basiert auf [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/de/1.0.0/),
und dieses Projekt folgt [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/lang/de/).

> **Hinweis:** Dieser Changelog wird automatisch bei jeder Г„nderung aktualisiert.

---

## [Unreleased]

### Added
- **tests: resolve 3 xfail TP/SL markers + add unit coverage for affiliate fetcher, funding tracker, Telegram poller, and HL/risk-state dependencies** вҖ” All three `@pytest.mark.xfail` markers in `tests/unit/bot/test_tpsl_passthrough.py:263` and `tests/integration/test_tpsl_flow.py:274/618` were test drift (not production bugs): mock trade records lacked explicit `trailing_atr_override=None` and `native_trailing_stop=False`, causing the position-monitor's `has_trailing` guard to evaluate truthy on `MagicMock` attributes. Additionally, strategy mocks needed `_p = {"trailing_stop_enabled": False}` to prevent the trailing-stop code path from overriding the exchange-TP/SL skip. All 3 markers removed; all 14 previously-xfail tests now pass. New test files added: `tests/unit/services/test_affiliate_revenue_fetcher.py` (25 tests), `tests/unit/data/test_funding_tracker.py` (25 tests), `tests/unit/telegram/test_poller.py` (21 tests), `tests/unit/api/dependencies/test_risk_state.py` (14 tests), `tests/unit/api/dependencies/test_hl_trailing.py` (6 tests). Total: 91 new test functions across 5 modules.


- **docs(observability): bilingual operator guide for Prometheus Alertmanager wiring (#216 Phase 2.3)** вҖ” New `Anleitungen/monitoring_alerts_setup.md` (DE/EN). Closes the operator-docs gap around the 16 infra alert rules in `monitoring/alert_rules.yml`: how to verify Prometheus loaded the rules post-deploy, how to add the Alertmanager service to `docker-compose.monitoring.yml`, step-by-step Discord webhook setup with an end-to-end `curl`-based test, Telegram options (dedicated proxy or reuse of the app webhook), a per-alert severity + typical-fix table for all 16 rules, and a troubleshooting section covering the common "alert firing but no message" causes. Complements the existing `observability_setup.md` (which covers Prometheus/Grafana auto-provisioning) and disambiguates from `Alerts-einrichten.md` (in-app user-facing price/strategy alerts) with a scope banner at the top.

### Fixed
- **fix(ws): route Bitget private WebSocket to demo host when `demo_mode=True` (#357)** вҖ” `BitgetWebSocketClient.__init__` accepted `demo_mode` and stored it on the instance but never consulted it when choosing the WS URL: `self._ws_url = ws_url or WS_PRIVATE_URL` always resolved to the live host `wss://ws.bitget.com`. Demo-only users (users 1, 4, 10 post-2026-04-21 deploy) dialed live WS with demo credentials and Bitget rejected the login with `code=30017` ("Session invalid"), spamming `RSM exchange ws auth failed` every ~8 s per affected user вҖ” the rest of the bot kept working (polling path) but the push channel was dead. Root cause: REST uses a `paptrading: 1` header to hit demo through the same `api.bitget.com`, so the WS side inherited the incorrect assumption that one URL serves both modes. Actually demo WS has dedicated hosts (`wspap.bitget.com`), documented in Bitget's demo-trading WS docs. Fix: added `WS_PUBLIC_URL_DEMO` + `WS_PRIVATE_URL_DEMO` constants to `src/exchanges/bitget/constants.py` (with a comment calling out why the REST `paptrading` header doesn't transfer) and rewrote URL resolution in `src/exchanges/websockets/bitget_ws.py` to `self._ws_url = ws_url or (WS_PRIVATE_URL_DEMO if demo_mode else WS_PRIVATE_URL)`. Explicit `ws_url` still wins (tests / one-off routing). New unit test `tests/unit/exchanges/test_bitget_ws.py` locks down all three branches (demo вҶ’ demo host, live вҶ’ live host, explicit override sticks). Closes #357.
- **ci(tests): scope PostgreSQL step to `tests/integration/` + raise `max_connections` to 500 via docker exec (#354)** вҖ” Root cause of the PG pool exhaustion tracked in #354: the step ran `pytest tests/` against Postgres, so all ~150 unit-test files that use the central `test_engine` fixture (which honours `TEST_DATABASE_URL`) each spun up a function-scoped async engine against the shared `postgres:16-alpine` service вҖ” which ships with `max_connections=100` by default. Even with `NullPool`, pytest-asyncio 1.x `auto` mode creates one event loop per test and `engine.dispose()` occasionally failed to release connections before the loop closed (`RuntimeError: Event loop is closed` spam + `FATAL: sorry, too many clients already`), stalling the step at the 5-min step timeout added as mitigation under #352. Three changes: (1) `.github/workflows/ci.yml` вҖ” the PG step now runs `pytest tests/integration/` (17 files / 237 tests) instead of `pytest tests/` (150+ files / 3800+ tests); unit tests don't exercise Postgres-specific behaviour (JSONB, migrations, concurrent transactions) and are fully covered by the authoritative SQLite step. Dropped `continue-on-error: true` and bumped `timeout-minutes` from 5 вҶ’ 10. (2) Added a setup step that execs into the running postgres container, appends `max_connections = 500` to `/var/lib/postgresql/data/postgresql.conf`, and restarts the container вҖ” GitHub Actions `services.postgres.options` cannot pass `-c` server flags (those are CMD args, not docker-create flags; see the `fec45a6` revert), so docker-level exec + restart is the only reliable path. (3) Reduced the production pool config during the PG step from `DB_POOL_SIZE=5/DB_MAX_OVERFLOW=10` to `2/3` so the FastAPI lifespan's `init_db` engine holds at most 5 connections per test, not 15. Verified locally: full integration suite `pytest tests/integration/ --timeout=120` reports `202 passed, 5 xfailed, 7 xpassed` in ~1m47s. Closes #354.
- **tests(ws): mock `get_session` instead of spinning up a real aiosqlite engine per test (#352, follow-up 3)** вҖ” `test_websocket_auth.py` had been flaking on CI: `test_ws_connect_with_unknown_user_is_rejected` intermittently hung at `starlette.testclient`'s `thread.join()` call, timing out at the 120 s pytest-timeout. Root cause: the fixture created a fresh `sqlite+aiosqlite:///:memory:` engine on a dedicated event loop for setup/teardown, while starlette's TestClient runs the WS handler inside its own portal thread with a separate loop. When the handler issued `async with get_session()` the aiosqlite connection was bound to starlette's loop; at test teardown the fixture's own loop called `engine.dispose()`, which blocked waiting to clean up connections owned by the already-closed starlette loop, keeping the portal thread alive forever. Rewrote the fixture to monkeypatch `src.api.routers.websocket.get_session` with an `@asynccontextmanager` that yields a `MagicMock` session; `session.execute(stmt)` inspects the compiled WHERE clause and returns the canned active user (`id=1`) or `None` (unknown-user path). No real engine, no cross-loop connection leakage, no thread-join hang. Side benefit: the whole test file runs in ~0.3 s (was ~2вҖ“3 s).
- **ci(tests): mark PostgreSQL pytest step non-blocking pending #354 (#352, follow-up 2)** вҖ” The `backend-tests` job runs pytest twice: once with SQLite, then once with PostgreSQL. Both steps were hidden until #352 because SQLite exited non-zero and the PG step was skipped. With SQLite now green, the PG step surfaced as its own failure: runs ~4Г— slower than SQLite (reached only 29 % of the suite in 8 min), exhausts the Postgres container's default `max_connections=100` (`FATAL: sorry, too many clients already` spammed from 13:36 onward), and emits `RuntimeError: Event loop is closed` tracebacks across many tests because pytest-asyncio 1.x auto mode tears down each loop before SQLAlchemy can dispose the async engine. The previous `-c max_connections=200` override in `ci.yml` was reverted in `fec45a6` with no replacement. Marked the PG step `continue-on-error: true` so the SQLite run (authoritative) restores a green `backend-tests` status. The PG step still executes and logs for diagnostic purposes. Full fix вҖ” pool sizing, engine disposal, or `max_connections` increase вҖ” tracked in #354; when resolved, drop `continue-on-error`.
- **ci(tests): patch `MarketDataFetcher` at service import site in 5 trailing-stop tests (#352, follow-up)** вҖ” After the 6-file fix dropped CI from 105 failures to 5, a new test-local discrepancy surfaced: `test_trailing_stop_long_active`, `test_trailing_stop_short_active`, `test_trailing_stop_not_active_when_not_profitable` (in `test_trades_router_extra.py`) and `test_get_trade_with_trailing_strategy_long_active_branch`, `test_get_trade_with_trailing_strategy_short_active_branch` (in `test_trades_router_characterization.py`) patched only `src.api.routers.trades.MarketDataFetcher`. The `_compute_trailing_stop` helper was moved to `src.services.trades_service` in #325 PR-1 and imports `MarketDataFetcher` from there, so the mock was bypassed. On Windows dev boxes the un-mocked path reached Binance and returned plausible klines (tests happened to pass); GitHub Actions runners get HTTP 451 (Binance geo-block) and the fetcher raised, dropping `trailing_stop_active` to `False`. Added `patch("src.services.trades_service.MarketDataFetcher", mock_cls)` alongside the existing router patch in all 5 tests, matching the pattern already used by `test_trailing_stop_in_list_trades` and `test_trailing_stop_kline_fetch_failure`. Also rewrote the two characterization tests' mock construction to build `mdf_cls = MagicMock(return_value=fetcher_mock)` explicitly so the same mock instance is installed at both import sites.
- **ci(tests): unblock 105 pre-existing `backend-tests` failures (#352)** вҖ” `backend-tests` had been red on `main` for 15+ consecutive runs with the same `105 failed, 3761 passed, 24 skipped, 6 xfailed, 8 xpassed, 6 errors` signature since the first red run `7fb4463` on 2026-04-23 (last green: `77b6b4d`, 2026-04-23 10:29:58Z). Every failure was a test-side drift against production code that had evolved cleanly, not a production regression вҖ” so the fix is purely in `tests/`. Five independent root causes addressed: (1) **91Г— integration failures** (`tests/integration/test_bots.py`, `test_trades.py`, `test_statistics.py`, `test_portfolio_router_characterization.py`, `test_trades_router_characterization.py`, `test_config_api.py`, `test_security_302.py`, `test_manual_close_full_flow.py`, `test_auth_flow.py` вҖ” all `assert 401 == 200` or `assert None is not None`): `admin_token`/`user_token` fixtures in `tests/integration/conftest.py` and the `test_refresh_token` assertions still read `response.json()["access_token"]`, but SEC-012 moved access tokens to an httpOnly cookie вҖ” body `access_token` is always `None` now. Changed the fixtures to read `response.cookies.get("access_token")`, and reworked `test_refresh_token` to read the rotated token from the response cookie before passing it to `/api/auth/me`. (2) **6Г— `test_websocket_auth.py` setup errors** (`RuntimeError: There is no current event loop in thread 'MainThread'`): the `test_app` fixture called `asyncio.get_event_loop().run_until_complete(...)` to drive its async setup/teardown, but pytest-asyncio 1.x `auto` mode leaves MainThread without a default loop outside of test functions. Replaced with an explicit `asyncio.new_event_loop()` that is closed on teardown. (3) **5Г— `test_production_hardening.py::TestMetricsIPRestriction`** (`ImportError: cannot import name '_is_allowed' from 'src.api.routers.metrics'`): the IP-allowlist implementation was architecturally superseded by flag-gated 404 + HTTP Basic-Auth in #327 PR-1, and the new contract is already covered by `tests/unit/observability/test_metrics_endpoint.py`. Deleted the obsolete class, replaced with a pointer comment to the new test file. (4) **3Г— `test_bots_router.py::TestClosePositionClassifyClose`** (`TypeError: float() argument must be a string or a real number, not 'coroutine'`): the manual-close path in `bots_lifecycle.py` awaits `client.get_trade_total_fees(...)` and `client.get_funding_fees(...)` and synchronously calls `client.calculate_builder_fee(...)`, writing the results to `TradeRecord` columns. `_build_mock_client()` did not stub these methods, so `AsyncMock` auto-spawned child mocks that returned coroutines / MagicMocks, which then failed SQL binding. Added explicit `AsyncMock(return_value=0.5/0.1)` for the two awaited fee fetchers, `MagicMock(return_value=0.0)` for the synchronous `calculate_builder_fee`, and `close_result.order_id = "manual_close_fill_001"` so the MagicMock's `.order_id` attribute is a real string. (5) **1Г— `test_validate_jwt_config_short_key`** (`AttributeError: module 'src.auth.jwt_handler' has no attribute '_get_secret_key'`): the function was renamed to `_get_hs_secret` in the RS256 + dual-validate refactor (#256). Removed the obsolete `patch("..._get_secret_key", ...)` and added `JWT_PRIVATE_KEY`/`JWT_PUBLIC_KEY=""` to the `patch.dict` call so `validate_jwt_config` takes the HS256 branch and hits the short-key check directly from the env. Verified locally with the CI command вҖ” full suite `pytest tests/ --timeout=60` now reports `3867 passed, 24 skipped, 6 xfailed, 8 xpassed` in ~10 min. Only test files touched (`tests/integration/conftest.py`, `tests/integration/test_auth_flow.py`, `tests/unit/api/test_websocket_auth.py`, `tests/unit/api/test_bots_router.py`, `tests/unit/test_production_hardening.py`, `tests/unit/test_remaining_coverage.py`); zero production-code changes.
- **ci(lint): resolve pre-existing ruff violations blocking `lint` job (#345)** вҖ” 16Г— F401 unused imports removed across `src/api/middleware/metrics.py`, `src/api/routers/config_exchange.py`, `src/bot/components/risk/alert_throttler.py`, `src/exchanges/hyperliquid/client.py`, `src/risk/risk_manager.py`, `src/observability/metrics.py` (kept `CONTENT_TYPE_LATEST` with `# noqa: F401` вҖ” re-exported from `src/observability/__init__.py`), plus several test files. 2Г— E702 semicolon one-liners in `tests/unit/bot/test_risk_state_manager_characterization.py:474,744` split into two-statement lines. 1Г— F821 `Any` undefined in `tests/unit/services/test_bots_service.py:822` вҖ” added `from typing import Any`. Smoke-tested all import chains (`from src.api.main_app import app` clean). 129 tests across the touched modules pass. CI `lint` job now green; follow-up issue #346 tracks the separate `alembic-check` duplicate-025 failure.
- **ci(migrations): resolve duplicate 025 revision blocking alembic `upgrade head` (#346)** вҖ” Two migrations declared `revision="025"` with `down_revision="024"` (`025_add_session_version.py` from commit `6fec8e1` / PR #261, and `025_add_unique_exchange_order_id_to_trade_records.py` from commit `fd7e128` / PR #244), producing `FAILED: Multiple head revisions are present for given argument 'head'` on every `alembic upgrade head`. Renumbered the unique-order-id migration to `028` (chains after `027` soft-delete), leaving the `session_version` migration at `025`. Safe-renumber: both migrations were committed AFTER the last prod deploy (`fd77ba9` on 2026-04-21), so neither has been applied to any production DB вҖ” no `alembic stamp` reconciliation needed. Verified locally: `alembic heads` now reports a single head `028`, `alembic history` shows linear chain `023 вҶ’ 024 вҶ’ 025 вҶ’ 026 вҶ’ 027 вҶ’ 028`. Unblocks the heads-check step of `alembic-check`; a separate latent bug in migration 001's use of `Base.metadata.create_all()` still blocks the job from going fully green and is tracked as #350.
- **ci(migrations): migration 001 uses frozen 2026-02-19 schema instead of live ORM (#350)** вҖ” Migration `001_initial_schema.py` called `Base.metadata.create_all(bind=bind)` where `Base` was imported from the **live** `src.models.database`. On a fresh DB (CI `alembic-check`, new dev machines) this created the fully-evolved current schema in revision 001, then every subsequent `op.add_column()` in migrations 002..028 failed with `DuplicateColumnError: column "X" of relation "Y" already exists` (first casualty: migration 005 / `trade_records.native_trailing_stop`). Latent since the ORM first drifted past the 001 baseline (approximately migration 002). Fix: added `migrations/_initial_schema_models.py` as a **verbatim copy** of `src/models/database.py` at commit `0551c2c` (2026-02-19, the commit that introduced the Alembic framework), added empty `migrations/__init__.py` so the directory is importable, and rewrote `migrations/versions/001_initial_schema.py` to `from migrations._initial_schema_models import Base`. The live ORM is now decoupled from revision 001 вҖ” 001 creates only the 14 tables that existed at 2026-02-19 (not the 20+ current), and 002..028 apply their diffs cleanly. Verified locally on fresh SQLite: `alembic upgrade 001` creates 14 tables; `trade_records` has 29 columns (no `native_trailing_stop`, `risk_state_at_entry`, or `exchange_order_id`); `bot_configs` has no `margin_mode`; `alembic downgrade base` drops all tables cleanly. Prod DBs are unaffected (alembic_version already points past 001, so `upgrade` is a no-op there). Unblocks CI `alembic-check` to finally go green.

Inventory over 8 categories (TS strictness, API client integrity, state management, error boundaries, a11y, performance, theme+i18n, test coverage); 3 critical / 5 medium / 6 nice-to-have findings; 8 follow-up issues #329вҖ“#336 filed.
### Fixed
- **Align frontend `Trade` type with backend `TradeResponse` schema (#329, from audit #328)**: Closes the "API shape drift" red flag surfaced in the frontend audit. (1) Added `builder_fee: float = Field(default=0, ...)` to `src/api/schemas/trade.py::TradeResponse` вҖ” the field already existed on `TradeRecord` (`src/models/database.py:180`) and is written by `trade_closer`/`position_monitor` from Hyperliquid's `calculate_builder_fee`, but was never surfaced in the API response that the FE `Trade` type claimed it received. (2) Relaxed `frontend/src/types/index.ts::Trade.take_profit` and `stop_loss` from `number` to `number | null` to match the BE's `Optional[float]` вҖ” the bot worker creates trades without TP/SL and fills them post-entry, so the non-nullable FE type was incorrect. No consumer changes required: every call site (`pages/Trades.tsx`, `utils/riskState.ts`, `components/ui/EditPositionPanel.tsx`, `components/ui/MobilePositionCard.tsx`) already uses optional-chaining or nullish guards, so `npx tsc --noEmit` stays clean. New Pydantic tests in `tests/unit/api/test_schema_validation.py::TestTradeResponseContract` lock the four fields (builder_fee default, builder_fee value, nullable TP/SL, populated TP/SL); `test_trades_router.py::test_get_trade_all_fields_present` now asserts `builder_fee` is in the response and defaults to 0.
- `eslint-plugin-jsx-a11y` installed + configured (warn-level). Initial scan documented in frontend health report. Strict enforcement follows in #333 (#330, from audit #328).
- **Global unhandledrejection + error handler fГјr Telemetry und User-Feedback (#331)**: Neues Modul `frontend/src/lib/globalErrorHandler.ts` hГӨngt auf dem Top-Level `window`-Objekt die Listener `unhandledrejection` (unbehandelte Promise-Rejections вҖ” z. B. `fetch().then()` ohne `.catch`, fehlendes `await`) und `error` (unbeobachtete Exceptions aus async Event-Handlern, die oberhalb der React-`ErrorBoundary` geworfen werden). Pro Event: (1) strukturierter `console.error`-Log mit stabilem `[GlobalError]`-Tag und vollem Kontext (`source`, `message`, `stack`, `filename`, `lineno`, `colno`, `timestamp`) fГјr Entwickler; (2) User-sichtbarer Toast via die bestehende unified Toast-API (`showError` aus `frontend/src/utils/toast.ts` вҶ’ `useToastStore` вҶ’ `ToastContainer` in `App.tsx`); (3) `reportError(err, ctx)` Telemetry-Stub, der aktuell mit `[telemetry]`-PrГӨfix auf `console.info` emittiert und spГӨter auf Sentry/PostHog umgebogen wird (dependency-injection-ready вҖ” keine neuen Packages). (4) Burst-Dedupe: identische Messages innerhalb eines 5-Sekunden-Fensters erzeugen nur einen Toast + einen Telemetry-Call (der Dev-`console.error` feuert weiterhin jedes Mal, damit Debugging nicht leidet). Installation ist idempotent (zweiter Aufruf gibt dasselbe Handle zurГјck, keine Doppel-Bindung), SSR-safe (no-op wenn `window` fehlt), und robust (wenn der Telemetry-Sink selbst wirft, wird der Toast trotzdem angezeigt). Verdrahtet in `frontend/src/main.tsx` mit einem einzelnen `installGlobalErrorHandler()`-Aufruf VOR `ReactDOM.createRoot(...)`, damit auch async Failures wГӨhrend des initialen Renders (z. B. lazy-geladene Chunk-FehlschlГӨge) erfasst werden. Neue Test-Suite `frontend/src/lib/globalErrorHandler.test.ts` mit 8 Vitest-Tests auf jsdom: Unhandled-Rejection-Capture mit Toast + Telemetry, Window-`error`-Capture mit Source-Metadata (`filename`/`lineno`/`colno`), 5s-Dedupe innerhalb des Fensters mit korrekter Wiederfreigabe danach, distinkte Messages passieren ungehindert, Normalisierung von non-Error-Werten (String / Object / `null` вҶ’ `"Unknown error"`), Idempotenz (zweifaches Install bindet Listener nicht doppelt), `uninstall()` detacht beide Listener, und ein throwing-Telemetry-Sink blockiert den Toast nicht.
### Fixed
- **[frontend] setTimeout leak in Admin/Settings/Bots/BotPerformance (#332)**: All four audited pages scheduled one-shot `setTimeout` callbacks inside click handlers (showMessage banner reset in `Admin.tsx` + `Settings.tsx`, "copied" flag reset after clipboard/share in `Bots.tsx`'s `TradeDetailModal` and `BotPerformance.tsx`'s `handleShare`) without a matching `clearTimeout` on unmount. If the user navigated away or closed the modal within the 2вҖ“3 s window, the deferred `setMessage('')` / `setCopied(false)` / `setFlag(false)` fired against a stale component, producing React "state update on unmounted component" warnings (and, under StrictMode, double-invocation pressure). Each site now stores its handle in a `useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>`, clears a pre-existing handle before scheduling a new one (also prevents overlapping timers on rapid repeated calls), and a dedicated `useEffect` with empty deps clears the pending handle on unmount. Behaviour for in-flight lifecycles is unchanged. New regression tests in `frontend/src/pages/__tests__/Bots.test.tsx`, `Settings.test.tsx`, `BotPerformance.test.tsx` mount each page under `vi.useFakeTimers()`, unmount, run `vi.runAllTimers()`, and assert no `"can't perform a React state update on an unmounted"` warning is logged to `console.error`. `Admin.tsx` has no existing test file вҖ” not added (noted for follow-up).
### Documentation
- **Frontend: Rationale-Kommentare fГјr alle `eslint-disable react-hooks/exhaustive-deps`-Stellen (#336)**: Audit hatte fГјnf Stellen identifiziert, an denen die Regel ohne BegrГјndungskommentar deaktiviert war вҖ” jeder solche Disable ist eine Behauptung, dass der Linter an dieser Stelle falsch liegt, aber ohne Kommentar kann ein spГӨterer Maintainer nicht beurteilen, ob der Disable noch gГјltig oder stale ist. Dokumentations-only Г„nderung (keine Code-Semantik geГӨndert, keine Deps-Arrays modifiziert, keine Disables entfernt): (1) `frontend/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:36` вҖ” `useMemo(() => handlers, [handlerKeys])` keyt absichtlich auf dem sortierten Key-String statt auf der Handler-Objekt-IdentitГӨt; Caller Гјbergeben typisch frische Objekt-Literale, ein Include von `handlers` wГјrde den Memo zerstГ¶ren und bei jedem Parent-Render die WS-Verbindung neu aufbauen. (2) `frontend/src/components/bots/CopyTradingStepExchange.tsx:95` вҖ” Empty-deps Mount-once-Effekt setzt Sentinel-Trading-Pair; `onTradingPairsChange` ausgeschlossen, da Parent-Callback bei jedem Render neu erzeugt wird. (3) `frontend/src/pages/Dashboard.tsx:102` вҖ” Empty-deps, `syncTrades` (React-Query-Mutation) ausgeschlossen weil neue Referenz bei jedem Render; `sessionStorage`-Guard verhindert Mehrfach-Sync. (4) `frontend/src/pages/Trades.tsx:153` вҖ” Gleiche Rationale wie Dashboard. (5) `frontend/src/components/ui/GuidedTour.tsx:162` вҖ” `[isActive]` mit ausgeschlossenem `handleSkip`; plus `TODO(#336)` als Follow-up-Hinweis, dass ein sauberer Fix wГӨre, `handleSkip` in `useCallback` zu wrappen вҖ” heute risikoarm (stable Closures Гјber zustand-Setter + Props), aber der Disable versteckt einen latenten Stale-Closure-Hazard. Keine Regressions in 553 Vitest-Tests; TypeScript-Check sauber; Lint-Output fГјr die fГјnf geГӨnderten Files zeigt keine neuen Warnings/Errors (die pre-existing Errors sind unverwandt: `react-hooks/globals` in `Trades.test.tsx`, `react-hooks/refs` in `Dashboard.tsx`).
### Security
- **Dependency audit sweep (2026-04-24)**: Periodische Housekeeping-Runde vor dem pip-audit/npm-audit CI-Gate (#260). Backend (`pip-audit -r requirements.txt -r requirements-dev.txt`): **keine bekannten Schwachstellen** вҖ” alle Python-Floor-Versions (aiohttp вүҘ3.9, httpx вүҘ0.27, cryptography вүҘ42, PyJWT вүҘ2.8, fastapi вүҘ0.109, etc.) sind vuln-frei. Frontend (`npm audit` in `frontend/`): 13 moderate-severity Findings vor dem Fix вҶ’ `npm audit fix --legacy-peer-deps` (non-force) hat 2 Findings durch transitive Patches eliminiert (axios-Kette unter `@coinbase/cdp-sdk` von `1.13.6` auf gepinnte `1.15.2`; `@metamask/utils` auf `11.11.0`; `@coinbase/cdp-sdk` auf `1.48.2`; `viem` transitive auf `2.48.4`; `jose` auf `6.2.2`). Nur `frontend/package-lock.json` geГӨndert вҖ” `package.json` unberГјhrt, keine API-Surface-Г„nderung. **11 verbleibende Findings (alle moderate, alle transitive MetaMask/WalletConnect/Solana-AbhГӨngigkeiten von `wagmi`/`@rainbow-me/rainbowkit`)** werden von `npm audit` mit einer SemVer-Major-**Downgrade**-Empfehlung (`wagmi@3.6.4` statt aktuell `2.19.5`, `@rainbow-me/rainbowkit@2.0.8` statt `2.2.10`) gelabelt, d.h. keine sichere Auto-Anwendung mГ¶glich вҖ” als **manueller Follow-up** geflaggt. Frontend-Tests (553/553 grГјn, `vitest run`) und `tsc --noEmit` nach dem Fix sauber; Backend `tests/unit` unverГӨndert (Vorher/Nachher identisches Pass/Fail-Pattern, keine Dep-Regressionen).
### Accessibility
- **Keyboard-accessible click handlers on non-interactive elements (#333)**: Replaced or augmented every `onClick` on `<div>` / `<tr>` / similar non-interactive elements so that screen-reader and keyboard-only users can activate them. Approach per site: (a) single-purpose headers/backdrops converted to `<button type="button">` with unstyled visuals (`appearance-none bg-transparent border-0`) preserving existing layout; (b) table rows (`<tr>`) given `tabIndex={0}`, `aria-expanded`, and an `onKeyDown` that activates on Enter/Space вҖ” the implicit `row` role is retained so table semantics stay intact; (c) modal backdrops converted to overlay `<button>` with `tabIndex={-1}` and Escape handled by the inner `role="dialog"`; (d) `ConfirmModal` backdrop uses `role="presentation"` `<div>` with both `onClick` + `onKeyDown` so the existing focus-trap keeps only the 3 real buttons in the tab loop. Files touched: `frontend/src/pages/{Admin,AdminBroadcasts,Bots,BotPerformance,Dashboard,Portfolio,TaxReport,Trades}.tsx`, `frontend/src/components/layout/MobileBottomNav.tsx`, `frontend/src/components/ui/{ConfirmModal,EditPositionPanel,GuidedTour}.tsx`. No visual or behavioral regressions вҖ” all 553 frontend tests pass. Lint totals unchanged (pre-existing 18 errors / 76 warnings). No changes to `.eslintrc.cjs` or `package.json`.
### Tooling
- **Frontend: Coverage-Skript + erzwungene Schwellen (#334)**: `frontend/package.json` bekommt ein neues Script `test:coverage` (`vitest run --coverage`), das `@vitest/coverage-v8@^4.0.18` (synchronisiert auf `vitest@4.0.18`, damit `vitest/node`-Exports matchen) als Dev-Dep pinnt. `frontend/vitest.config.ts` konfiguriert den `v8`-Provider mit den Reportern `text` / `html` / `lcov`, `include: ['src/**/*.{ts,tsx}']` und einer Exclude-Liste fГјr `*.d.ts`, Test-Dateien, `src/main.tsx`, `src/vite-env.d.ts` und `src/test/**`. Thresholds als Regressions-Floor: Statements вүҘ 42 %, Branches вүҘ 30 %, Functions вүҘ 37 %, Lines вүҘ 42 % вҖ” jeweils 2вҖ“4 Punkte unter dem Ist-Stand (44.09 / 32.97 / 40.19 / 45.75 %) laut erstem Lauf. `testTimeout` global von 5 s auf 20 s angehoben, weil v8-Instrumentierung den parallelen Trades-Virtualisierungs-Test (`src/pages/__tests__/Trades.test.tsx`) Гјber den Default-Timeout hinaus bremst; ohne Coverage bleibt `npm test` davon unberГјhrt (alle 553 Tests laufen weiterhin durch). Neues `frontend/.gitignore` schlieГҹt `coverage/` + `*.lcov` vom Commit aus. Anleitung `Anleitungen/frontend-testing.md` dokumentiert bilingual (DE + EN) Scripts, Reports, Threshold-Anhebung und den `--legacy-peer-deps`-Installationsschritt (analog zur CI).
- **Playwright E2E smoke tests for frontend (#335)**: New Playwright-based end-to-end test harness in `frontend/e2e/` covering three critical flows вҖ” login (`login.spec.ts`), bot create wizard (`bot-create.spec.ts`), and manual position close (`manual-close.spec.ts`). Each spec ships an env-free subtest (form renders / auth guard redirects) plus a credential-driven subtest that self-skips when `E2E_USER` / `E2E_PASS` are not set вҖ” never fails CI due to missing secrets. Playwright config (`frontend/playwright.config.ts`) uses a `setup` project (`e2e/global.setup.ts`) to perform a single login and persist `storageState` to `frontend/e2e/.auth/user.json`, which is reused by all authenticated specs. `webServer` block starts `npm run dev` automatically with a 120 s timeout. Chromium only (keeps CI runtime down). New npm scripts `test:e2e` / `test:e2e:headed`. New non-blocking CI job `frontend-e2e` in `.github/workflows/ci.yml` (`continue-on-error: true` until the suite is flake-proven) that installs Chromium, runs the suite, and uploads `playwright-report/` as an artifact (7-day retention). Frontend `.gitignore` created to exclude `test-results/`, `playwright-report/`, `.playwright/`, `e2e/.auth/`. Required GitHub Secrets for the full flow: `E2E_USER`, `E2E_PASS`, optional `E2E_HAS_OPEN_TRADE`. Bilingual DE/EN guide in `Anleitungen/frontend-e2e-playwright.md`.

### Refactored
- **ARCH-H2 Phase 2 PR-8: Finalize `RiskManager` composition faГ§ade, remove Phase 1 backward-compat shims (#339, #326 PR-8)**: Abschluss-PR fГјr die `src/risk/risk_manager.py`-Kompositionsarbeit (#326). Entfernt drei RГјckwГӨrtskompat-Property-Shims aus dem `RiskManager`-FaГ§ade, die in Phase 1 (PR-5 / PR-6 / PR-7) eingezogen wurden, um die Extraktionen von `DailyStatsAggregator`, `TradeGate` und `RiskStatePersistence` ohne Call-Site-Migrationen durchzuziehen: (1) `@property _daily_stats` / `@setter _daily_stats` leiteten auf `self._daily_stats_aggregator.get_daily_stats()` bzw. `self._daily_stats_aggregator.hydrate()` um; (2) `def _halt_trading(reason)` leitete auf `self._trade_gate._halt_trading(reason)` um; (3) `@property halted_symbols` leitete auf `self._trade_gate.halted_symbols` um. Parallel fallen die beiden `AlertThrottler`-Shims aus `src/bot/bot_worker.py` weg: `@property _risk_alerts_sent` / `@setter` (вҶ’ `self._alert_throttler.sent`) und `@property _risk_alerts_last_reset` / `@setter` (вҶ’ `self._alert_throttler.last_reset`). Interne `self._daily_stats`-Lesestellen im FaГ§ade selbst wurden auf `self._daily_stats_aggregator.get_daily_stats()` umgeschrieben. Produktionsaufrufer `src/api/routers/bots_lifecycle.py:551` (manueller Close-Pfad) wurde auf `risk_manager.get_daily_stats()` migriert вҖ” war der einzige Nicht-Test-Konsument der alten Attribut-Form. Test-Migrationen (Nicht-Shim-Benutzer-Seite): `tests/unit/test_risk_manager.py` (5 Call-Sites: 4Г— `rm._daily_stats = None` вҶ’ `rm._daily_stats_aggregator = DailyStatsAggregator()`, 3Г— `rm._halt_trading(...)` вҶ’ `rm._trade_gate._halt_trading(...)`); `tests/unit/observability/test_risk_instrumentation.py` (8 Call-Sites: `rm._daily_stats.<field>` вҶ’ `rm._daily_stats_aggregator.get_daily_stats().<field>`); `tests/unit/bot/test_risk_state_manager_characterization.py` (11 Call-Sites: `worker._risk_alerts_sent` вҶ’ `worker._alert_throttler.sent`, `worker._risk_alerts_last_reset` вҶ’ `worker._alert_throttler.last_reset`); `tests/unit/bot/test_bot_worker_daily_summary.py` (8 Call-Sites: dito); `tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_persistence.py` (1 Call-Site: `rm._daily_stats = _make_dailystats()` вҶ’ `rm._daily_stats_aggregator.hydrate(_make_dailystats())`); `tests/unit/test_remaining_coverage.py` (1 Call-Site: `rm._daily_stats = MagicMock()` вҶ’ `rm._daily_stats_aggregator = MagicMock(...)` mit `get_daily_stats.return_value`-Verdrahtung). `tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_trade_gate.py` bleibt **unberГјhrt** вҖ” der verwendete `gate.halted_symbols` + `gate._halt_trading` Pfad ist die **Komponenten-API** auf `TradeGate` selbst, keine FaГ§ade-Shim. `src/risk/risk_manager.py` jetzt **295 LOC** (Ziel <200 LOC verfehlt um 95 LOC; alle Methoden sind dГјnne Delegatoren, ohne weitere Komponenten-Extraktion kein tieferer Trim mГ¶glich вҖ” documented). `src/bot/bot_worker.py`: 14 LOC entfernt (5 Property-Definitionen fГјr die zwei Shim-Paare) + Kommentar-Update. Null VerhaltensГӨnderung fГјr externe Konsumenten (nur die interne FaГ§ade-OberflГӨche ist ГӨndert). 0 Prod-Call-Sites mehr, die auf die alten Shims referenzieren.

- **ARCH-C1 Phase 2a PR-3: Finalize TradesService extraction, trim `trades` router under 400 LOC (#325 PR-3)**: Cleanup/Finalize-Commit fГјr den ARCH-C1-Stack. `src/api/routers/trades.py` ist jetzt ein reiner FastAPI-Adapter вҖ” **652 вҶ’ 326 LOC** (-326, unter dem 400-LOC-Gate aus `coding-style.md`). Was noch im Router lebt: die sechs Route-Handler, das Feature-Flag-Gate und das Exception-Mapping auf HTTP-Statuscodes. Was aus dem Router verschwunden ist: (a) `_compute_trailing_stop` + `TRAILING_STOP_STRATEGIES` Konstante (lebten seit PR-2 in `src/services/trades_service.py`, werden jetzt nur noch dort gepflegt вҖ” externe Konsumenten `src/api/routers/bots_statistics.py:15` und `tests/unit/test_resolve_strategy_params.py` (5 Import-Sites) wurden auf den Service-Pfad umgezogen); (b) die vier inline-Pydantic-Modelle `TrailingStopParams`, `UpdateTpSlRequest`, `RiskLegStatus`, `TpSlResponse` sind jetzt in `src/api/schemas/trade.py` gesammelt вҖ” ein Modul pro HTTP-Namespace, analog zu den anderen Routern; (c) die Hilfs-Mapper `_outcome_to_status`, `_leg_snapshot_to_status`, `_intent_from_body`, `_invalid_intent_detail` und die drei Mapping-Konstanten (`_INVALID_INTENT_DETAIL`-Dict, `MUTEX_CONFLICT_REASONS`-Frozenset, `EXCHANGE_ERROR_HINTS`-Tuple) sind in das neue private Helper-Modul `src/api/routers/_trades_mappers.py` (113 LOC) gewandert. Der frГјhere Outcome/Snapshot-Duplikat wurde zu **einem** unified `leg_to_status(leg)`-Helper konsolidiert вҖ” `RiskLegOutcome` (Manager-Write-Pfad) und `RiskLegSnapshot` (Read-Pfad) haben identische Felder, also ist eine duck-typed Projektion korrekt. `trade_response(item)` nutzt jetzt `dataclasses.asdict(item)` + Spread der `trailing`-Dict-Keys fГјr eine saubere `TradeResponse`-Projektion ohne Attribut-Handpicking. Keine VerhaltensГӨnderung: Alle 61 Characterization-Tests aus #325 Phase 0 bleiben grГјn, Routen-Kontrakt ist identisch (gleiche HTTP-Codes, gleiche Response-Shapes, gleiche Fehler-Details). Zusatz: 3 orphan Integration-Tests in `tests/integration/test_tp_sl_endpoint_v2.py` вҖ” die in PR-2 durch das Migrieren von `_compute_atr_for_trailing`, `_derive_overall_status` und `RiskLegStatus` aus dem Router verwaist waren (`test_compute_atr_for_trailing_returns_live_value`, `test_compute_atr_for_trailing_falls_back_on_exception`, `test_derive_overall_status_edges`) вҖ” wurden im Zuge des Cleanups auf den Service-Import umgezogen (`from src.services.trades_service import _compute_atr_for_trailing, _derive_overall_status, RiskLegOutcome`) und laufen wieder grГјn. Damit schlieГҹt #325 den vollstГӨndigen Extract-Zyklus ab: Phase 0 Characterization (61 Tests) вҶ’ PR-1 Read-Handler вҶ’ PR-2 Write-Handler вҶ’ PR-3 Cleanup (Router 929 вҶ’ 326 LOC, -65%, -603 LOC Гјber den gesamten Stack).
- **ARCH-C1 Phase 2a PR-2: Extract write handlers from `trades` router into `TradesService` (#325 PR-2)**: `POST /api/trades/sync` und `PUT /api/trades/{trade_id}/tp-sl` sind jetzt dГјnne HTTP-Adapter. Die Business-Logik lebt in `src/services/trades_service.py` als drei neue FastAPI-freie Methoden: `TradesService.sync_exchange_positions(...) -> SyncResult` (iteriert offene Trades, closed vanished positions, Discord-Webhook side-effect, RSM-`reconcile` post-close), `TradesService.update_tp_sl_via_manager(trade_id, intent, ...) -> TpSlManagerResult` (RiskStateManager-Pfad mit per-leg try/except und Idempotency-Cache), und `TradesService.update_tp_sl_legacy(trade_id, intent, ...) -> TpSlLegacyResult` (direkte Exchange-Calls mit `with_for_update()` row-lock und ATR-Trailing). Router owned nur noch das Feature-Flag-Gate (`settings.risk.risk_state_manager_enabled`), Idempotency-Header-Parsing und Exception-Mapping (404 `TradeNotFound`, 400 `TradeNotOpen`, 400/422 `InvalidTpSlIntent` вҖ” 422 nur fГјr Mutex-Conflicts auf dem Manager-Pfad, 400 fГјr Preis/Side-Validation auf beiden Pfaden, 400 `ExchangeConnectionMissing`, 400 `TpSlExchangeNotSupported`, 400/502 `TpSlUpdateFailed` mit Exchange-Hint-Disambiguation via `translate_exchange_error`). Neue Domain-Exceptions in `src/services/exceptions.py`: `TradeNotOpen`, `ExchangeConnectionMissing`, `TpSlExchangeNotSupported`, `TpSlUpdateFailed`. Neue Dataclasses: `TpSlIntent` (Request-DTO), `RiskLegOutcome`, `TpSlManagerResult`, `TpSlLegacyResult`, `SyncClosedTrade`, `SyncResult`. Helper `_validate_tp_sl_against_trade`, `_compute_atr_for_trailing`, `_build_trailing_intent`, `_resolve_exit_reason`, `_send_sync_discord_notifications` in Service migriert. Externe AbhГӨngigkeiten (`decrypt_value`, `create_exchange_client`, `get_risk_state_manager`, `get_idempotency_cache`, `MarketDataFetcher`, `DiscordNotifier`) werden per DI als keyword-args an die Service-Methoden gereicht, damit die Phase-0-Characterization-Tests ihre `src.api.routers.trades.*`-Patches weiter durchreichen kГ¶nnen. `DiscordNotifier` wird on-call-time aus `src.notifications.discord_notifier` nachgelesen, damit der AttributePatch im Sync-Test greift. Router: **929 вҶ’ 652 LOC** (-277). Alle 61 Characterization-Tests aus #325 Phase 0 bleiben grГјn; 15 neue Service-Unit-Tests in `tests/unit/services/test_trades_service.py` decken Sync (happy path, no-open-trades, exchange-error swallowing), Manager-Pfad (happy path, idempotency cache hit, per-leg exception вҶ’ REJECTED + partial_success, TP-Conflict, TradeNotOpen, TradeNotFound) und Legacy-Pfad (happy path, missing connection, NotImplementedError, generic exception, side-violation, TradeNotFound) ab. `_compute_trailing_stop` + `TRAILING_STOP_STRATEGIES` bleiben vorlГӨufig im Router вҖ” sie werden in PR-3 (Cleanup) aufgerГӨumt.
- **ARCH-C1 Phase 2a PR-1: Extract read handlers from `trades` router into `TradesService` (#325 PR-1)**: `GET /api/trades/{trade_id}` und `GET /api/trades/{trade_id}/risk-state` sind jetzt dГјnne HTTP-Adapter. Die Business-Logik (Query + Ownership-Check + Trailing-Stop-Enrichment in `get_trade`; Ownership + `RiskStateManager.reconcile` + Leg-Snapshot-Aggregation in `get_risk_state_snapshot`) lebt in `src/services/trades_service.py` als `TradesService.get_trade(trade_id) -> TradeDetail` und `TradesService.get_risk_state_snapshot(trade_id, manager) -> RiskStateSnapshotResult`. Domain-Exception `TradeNotFound` (bereits in `src/services/exceptions.py` vorhanden) wird vom Router zu HTTP 404 gemappt; unbekannte und fremde Trades bleiben indistinguishable (Security-HГӨrtung, durch Characterization-Tests #325 Phase 0 eingefroren). Neue Ergebnis-Dataclasses: `TradeDetail`, `RiskLegSnapshot`, `RiskStateSnapshotResult` вҖ” router projiziert sie direkt auf die bestehenden Pydantic-Modelle (`TradeResponse`, `TpSlResponse`). Write-Handler (`sync_trades`, `update_trade_tpsl`) bleiben im Router und kommen in PR-2. Alle 61 Characterization-Tests aus #325 Phase 0 bleiben grГјn; 9 neue Service-Unit-Tests in `tests/unit/services/test_trades_service.py` decken Happy-Path, 404-Fusion, reconcile-ValueError-Mapping, no-legs вҶ’ `no_change` ab. `tests/unit/api/test_trades_router_extra.py::test_trailing_stop_kline_fetch_failure` wurde auf das Dual-Patch-Pattern umgestellt (`src.api.routers.trades.MarketDataFetcher` + `src.services.trades_service.MarketDataFetcher`), analog zu `test_trailing_stop_in_list_trades` nach #255.
- **ARCH-H2 Phase 1 PR-4: Extract `AlertThrottler` from `BotWorker` (#326)**: Dedupe-Set + Midnight-Reset-Logik + Notifier-Dispatch fГјr Risk-Alerts ausgelagert aus `BotWorker._analyze_and_trade` (vorher inline Lines ~1037вҖ“1086) und den beiden BotWorker-Attributen `_risk_alerts_sent` / `_risk_alerts_last_reset` in die neue Komponente `src/bot/components/risk/alert_throttler.py` (`AlertThrottler`). Die Komponente satisfyt `AlertThrottlerProtocol` aus Phase 0 und bГјndelt vier Verantwortungen: (1) Keyword-Filter (`"halted"` / `"limit"` Reasons werden geemittiert, sonst nicht), (2) Dedupe nach `alert_key`, (3) `TRADE_LIMIT` vs. `DAILY_LOSS_LIMIT` Klassifikation, (4) Notifier-Dispatch. High-Level-Helper `emit_global_if_needed(reason)` und `emit_per_symbol_if_needed(symbol, reason)` ersetzen die inlined `if alert_key not in self._risk_alerts_sent: ...`-BlГ¶cke. `BotWorker.__init__` konstruiert zusГӨtzlich `RiskComponentDeps` (aus Phase 0) und wired `_send_notification` via Thunk, damit Tests, die `worker._send_notification = AsyncMock()` nach Konstruktion setzen, weiterhin durchrouten. Backward-Compat: `BotWorker._risk_alerts_sent` + `_risk_alerts_last_reset` bleiben als Properties mit Getter/Setter erhalten, delegieren auf den Throttler вҖ” alle existierenden Characterization-Tests bleiben grГјn, ohne Anpassung. **Eine VerhaltensГӨnderung**: Notifier-Exceptions (Discord 500, Telegram-Timeout etc.) propagieren nicht mehr aus `_analyze_and_trade`; `AlertThrottler._dispatch` wrappt den Call in try/except und loggt eine Warning, sodass ein flakiger Webhook nie den Per-Symbol-Analyse-Loop killt. Der Phase-0 FIXME-Test `test_notifier_exception_does_not_break_analysis_loop` ist von `pytest.skip` auf grГјn geflippt und dokumentiert den neuen Swallow-Contract. **26 neue Unit-Tests** in `tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_alert_throttler.py` decken Protocol-Conformance, `should_emit` Dedupe, `maybe_reset` / `reset` Semantik (inkl. Invariante dass `reset()` den Timestamp NICHT bumpt, nur `maybe_reset()`), `emit_global_if_needed` / `emit_per_symbol_if_needed` Happy-Path + Dedupe + Key-Format + Skip-Non-Matching-Reason, Alert-Type-Classification (`TRADE_LIMIT` / `DAILY_LOSS_LIMIT`), Notifier-Exception-Swallow (global + per-symbol + key-bleibt-recordet-trotz-Exception) und Backward-Compat-Accessors (`sent` / `last_reset` Getter+Setter). Alle 42 bestehenden Characterization-Tests in `test_risk_state_manager_characterization.py` bleiben grГјn; Coverage `src/risk/risk_manager.py` stabil bei 86% (вүҘ85% Gate). 183 BotWorker-Unit-Tests, 119 Components-Unit-Tests, 409 gesamte `tests/unit/bot/` alle grГјn.

### Tests
- **ARCH-H2 Phase 0 sub-PR-2 + sub-PR-3: Characterization-Tests fГјr `RiskStateManager` (#326)**: Neuer Test-Modul `tests/unit/bot/test_risk_state_manager_characterization.py` friert das observable Verhalten der vier Risk-State-Verantwortungsbereiche ein, bevor in Phase 1 die Extraktion beginnt. **50 Tests** (+ 1 skipped, siehe unten) decken ab: (A) `get_daily_stats` вҖ” leere Shape, Win/Loss-Aggregation, `net_pnl`-Funding-Semantik, Same-Day-Idempotenz; (B) alle 8 `can_trade`-Branches (uninitialisiert, allow, no-limits, global-max-trades, global-daily-loss + `_halt_trading`-Side-Effect, `is_trading_halted`-Short-Circuit, per-symbol max-trades, per-symbol loss-limit mit `halted_symbols`-Mutation, per-symbol-override-Precedence); (C) Alert-Throttling Dedupe (erste Emission recordet Key, Duplicate dedupt, andere Reason emittiert, Non-`halted`/`limit` Reasons NICHT queued, per-symbol Key-Format `f"{symbol}_{reason}"`); (D) Midnight-Reset (24h-Window-Preservation, Reset + Timestamp-Bump nach >24h, Reset entsperrt Same-Key-Emission, `_send_daily_summary` unbedingter Reset); (E) DB-Lade-Pfad (#188 Truth-Source: disabled No-Op, Happy-Path Load mit Computed-Fields-Strip, Missing-Row-Leaves-None, Exception-Swallow); (F) Save-Path Happy + Swallow; (G) Aggregator Error-Paths (`record_entry`/`record_exit` vor Init вҶ’ False, `_save_daily_stats` No-Op, Profit-Lock negative-return Early-Return); (H) `TradeGate` Aux-Observables (`get_remaining_trades` 999-Sentinel + per-symbol, `get_remaining_risk_budget` None/full/decrement, `get_dynamic_loss_limit` None/disabled/tightens-after-profit); (I) `can_trade` recompute-and-halt-on-gate-side (Branch 357-367). Coverage auf `src/risk/risk_manager.py`: **77% вҶ’ 86%** (вүҘ85%-Gate erreicht). Verbleibende ungedeckte Zeilen sind out-of-scope: `calculate_position_size` (Lines 413-443, gehГ¶rt zu einer Future-`PositionSizer`-Komponente, nicht Phase 0/1) und `get_performance_summary` (Lines 638-668, Reports-Modul). 1 Test (`test_notifier_exception_does_not_break_analysis_loop`) dokumentiert als Surprise-Finding: der aktuelle `_analyze_and_trade`-Alert-Emission-Block wrappt `_send_notification` NICHT in try/except, ein fehlschlagender Notifier propagiert aus dem Analysis-Loop вҖ” Phase 1 `AlertThrottler` sollte das explizit wrappen. Test ist als `pytest.skip` mit FIXME-BegrГјndung belassen (freezing existing behaviour, not asserting it).

### Refactored
- **ARCH-H2 Phase 1 PR-5: Extract `DailyStatsAggregator` aus `RiskManager` (#326)**: Die mutable `DailyStats`-Snapshot-Verwaltung zieht vollstГӨndig in die neue `DailyStatsAggregator`-Komponente (`src/bot/components/risk/daily_stats.py`) um. Extrahiert wurden: (a) die `DailyStats`-Dataclass mit den drei `@property`-Computed-Fields (`net_pnl`, `return_percent`, `win_rate`) und `to_dict()`, (b) `initialize_day()` mit Same-Day-Idempotenz (Midnight-Reset-Trigger bleibt in der Bot-Worker-Schleife, wie von Phase-0-Characterization-Test `test_initialize_day_same_day_is_idempotent` eingefroren), (c) die Pure-State-Primitives `record_entry(symbol)` (inkrementiert `trades_executed` + `symbol_trades`) und `record_exit(side, size, entry_price, exit_price, fees, funding_paid)` (PnL/Fees/Funding-Akkumulation, Win/Loss-Counter, Max-Drawdown-Tracking, Per-Symbol-PnL), (d) der DB-Load-Strip-Helper `hydrate_from_dict()` als Static-Method, der die drei `@property`-Computed-Fields aus dem persisted Dict entfernt, bevor `DailyStats(**data)` konstruiert wird вҖ” ohne den Strip wГјrde der Dataclass-Constructor `TypeError: unexpected keyword argument 'net_pnl'` werfen (Contract gelockt durch neuen Test `test_strips_net_pnl_before_constructor`). `RiskManager` wird zum dГјnnen Delegator: das Feld `_daily_stats` ist jetzt eine `@property` (Getter/Setter) die auf den internen `_daily_stats_aggregator` forwarded вҖ” dadurch bleiben alle Call-Sites rГјckwГӨrtskompatibel (`self._daily_stats.trades_executed += 1` etc.), inklusive der `TradeGate`-Loss-Limit-Gates in `record_trade_exit`, die in Phase 1 PR-6 extrahiert werden. `from src.risk.risk_manager import DailyStats` funktioniert weiterhin (via Re-Export am Bottom-of-File вҖ” deferred Import lГ¶st den Zirkularimport `src.risk.risk_manager вҶ’ src.bot.components.risk.daily_stats вҶ’ src.bot.__init__ вҶ’ BotWorker вҶ’ RiskManager`). Zero Behaviour-Change: alle 50 Phase-0-Characterization-Tests (`tests/unit/bot/test_risk_state_manager_characterization.py`) bleiben grГјn, `tests/unit/test_risk_manager.py` (110 Tests) ebenfalls. Neuer Test-Modul `tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_daily_stats.py` mit 30 fokussierten Unit-Tests: Computed-Fields (7), Aggregator-Lifecycle + Idempotenz (6), record_entry (2), record_exit inkl. Short-Side-Inversion + Per-Symbol-Accumulation (7), DB-Load-Strip + Round-Trip (4), FaГ§ade-Delegation (4). Coverage: `src/bot/components/risk/daily_stats.py` **100%**, `src/risk/risk_manager.py` **86% вҶ’ 93%** (kombiniert 95%). Dateien: `src/bot/components/risk/daily_stats.py` 30 вҶ’ 274 Zeilen (+244), `src/risk/risk_manager.py` -97 Zeilen (DailyStats-Dataclass + direkte Mutation raus, Property-Delegator rein), neuer Test-File 330 Zeilen.

### Tests
- **ARCH-H2 Phase 0 sub-PR-2 + sub-PR-3: Characterization-Tests fГјr `RiskStateManager` (#326)**: Neuer Test-Modul `tests/unit/bot/test_risk_state_manager_characterization.py` friert das observable Verhalten der vier Risk-State-Verantwortungsbereiche ein, bevor in Phase 1 die Extraktion beginnt. **50 Tests** (+ 1 skipped, siehe unten) decken ab: (A) `get_daily_stats` вҖ” leere Shape, Win/Loss-Aggregation, `net_pnl`-Funding-Semantik, Same-Day-Idempotenz; (B) alle 8 `can_trade`-Branches (uninitialisiert, allow, no-limits, global-max-trades, global-daily-loss + `_halt_trading`-Side-Effect, `is_trading_halted`-Short-Circuit, per-symbol max-trades, per-symbol loss-limit mit `halted_symbols`-Mutation, per-symbol-override-Precedence); (C) Alert-Throttling Dedupe (erste Emission recordet Key, Duplicate dedupt, andere Reason emittiert, Non-`halted`/`limit` Reasons NICHT queued, per-symbol Key-Format `f"{symbol}_{reason}"`); (D) Midnight-Reset (24h-Window-Preservation, Reset + Timestamp-Bump nach >24h, Reset entsperrt Same-Key-Emission, `_send_daily_summary` unbedingter Reset); (E) DB-Lade-Pfad (#188 Truth-Source: disabled No-Op, Happy-Path Load mit Computed-Fields-Strip, Missing-Row-Leaves-None, Exception-Swallow); (F) Save-Path Happy + Swallow; (G) Aggregator Error-Paths (`record_entry`/`record_exit` vor Init вҶ’ False, `_save_daily_stats` No-Op, Profit-Lock negative-return Early-Return); (H) `TradeGate` Aux-Observables (`get_remaining_trades` 999-Sentinel + per-symbol, `get_remaining_risk_budget` None/full/decrement, `get_dynamic_loss_limit` None/disabled/tightens-after-profit); (I) `can_trade` recompute-and-halt-on-gate-side (Branch 357-367). Coverage auf `src/risk/risk_manager.py`: **77% вҶ’ 86%** (вүҘ85%-Gate erreicht). Verbleibende ungedeckte Zeilen sind out-of-scope: `calculate_position_size` (Lines 413-443, gehГ¶rt zu einer Future-`PositionSizer`-Komponente, nicht Phase 0/1) und `get_performance_summary` (Lines 638-668, Reports-Modul). 1 Test (`test_notifier_exception_does_not_break_analysis_loop`) dokumentiert als Surprise-Finding: der aktuelle `_analyze_and_trade`-Alert-Emission-Block wrappt `_send_notification` NICHT in try/except, ein fehlschlagender Notifier propagiert aus dem Analysis-Loop вҖ” Phase 1 `AlertThrottler` sollte das explizit wrappen. Test ist als `pytest.skip` mit FIXME-BegrГјndung belassen (freezing existing behaviour, not asserting it).

### Refactored
- **ARCH-H2 Phase 1 PR-6: Extract `TradeGate` aus `RiskManager` (#326)**: Die `can_trade()`-Gating-Logik + Halt-State-Verwaltung zieht vollstГӨndig in die neue `TradeGate`-Komponente (`src/bot/components/risk/trade_gate.py`, 325 Zeilen) um. Extrahiert wurden: (a) `can_trade(symbol)` mit allen 8 Branches (global-halt Short-Circuit, per-symbol pre-halted, per-symbol max-trades, per-symbol loss-limit lazy-halt, global max-trades, global daily-loss-limit + `_halt_trading`-Side-Effect, `Trading allowed`-Happy-Path, uninitialisierter Early-Return), (b) das globale Halt-Primitiv `_halt_trading(reason)` (setzt `is_trading_halted=True` + `halt_reason`), (c) der Profit-Lock-In Dynamic-Loss-Limit-Rechner `get_dynamic_loss_limit()` (Floor bei 0.5%, tightens nach Profit), (d) die Observability-Accessors `get_remaining_trades(symbol)` (999-Sentinel wenn kein Cap konfiguriert) + `get_remaining_risk_budget()`. **Eager/Lazy-Halt-Konsolidierung (Phase-0-Finding):** die Per-Symbol-Loss-Halt-Logik existierte bisher zweimal вҖ” eager in `record_trade_exit` (Zeilen 573-582 vor Extraktion) direkt nach PnL-Aufzeichnung, und lazy in `can_trade` (Zeilen 357-367) bei Aufruf mit Symbol. Beide Pfade konvergieren jetzt in `TradeGate`: `check_and_halt(symbol)` implementiert den eager-Pfad mit der Legacy-Wording-Variante (`Loss limit reached: X%`), der lazy-Pfad innerhalb `can_trade` behГӨlt die Legacy-Wording-Variante (`Loss limit exceeded (X% >= Y%)`) вҖ” beide Wordings byte-identisch zur Pre-Extraktions-Implementierung, Phase-0-Characterization-Test `test_can_trade_halts_on_pending_symbol_loss` deckt den Lazy-Pfad, `test_record_trade_exit_halts_symbol_on_loss_limit` den Eager-Pfad. `RiskManager` wird noch dГјnner: `can_trade` / `_halt_trading` / `get_dynamic_loss_limit` / `get_remaining_trades` / `get_remaining_risk_budget` sind jetzt One-Line-Delegator-Methoden; `halted_symbols` ist eine `@property`, die auf `TradeGate.halted_symbols` forwarded (Strategy aus PR-4 fГјr `_risk_alerts_sent` nachgezogen, erhГӨlt Reference-Semantics fГјr `rm.halted_symbols[sym] = ...`-Mutationen); der Eager-Halt-Block in `record_trade_exit` ist durch einen einzelnen `self._trade_gate.check_and_halt(symbol)`-Call ersetzt. Persistence-Write-Through geht unverГӨndert Гјber den `save_stats`-Callback, der bei der `TradeGate`-Konstruktion auf `self._save_daily_stats` gebunden wird. Zero Behaviour-Change: alle **50 Phase-0-Characterization-Tests** (`tests/unit/bot/test_risk_state_manager_characterization.py`) bleiben grГјn, alle **30 PR-5-Tests** (`tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_daily_stats.py`) bleiben grГјn, alle **110 Legacy-Tests** (`tests/unit/test_risk_manager.py`) bleiben grГјn. Neuer Test-Modul `tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_trade_gate.py` mit **36 fokussierten Unit-Tests**: Pre-Init-Observables (8), Global-Gating (6) inkl. Zero-Starting-Balance-Guard, Per-Symbol-Gating (4), **Eager/Lazy-Halt-Consolidation (5)** mit separaten Tests fГјr beide Pfade, Dynamic-Loss-Limit (6) inkl. Floor-at-0.5%, Remaining-Accessors (6) inkl. Clamp-to-Zero, Halted-Symbols-Proxy (1). Coverage: `src/bot/components/risk/trade_gate.py` **100%**, `src/risk/risk_manager.py` **90%** (kombiniert mit allen Risk-Tests; 93% vor PR-6 ist aufgrund des LOC-Abbaus leicht gesunken, Remaining-Branches sind Position-Sizing + Legacy-Sync-Historical-Stubs, out-of-scope). Datei-Deltas: `src/bot/components/risk/trade_gate.py` 13 вҶ’ 325 Zeilen (+312), `src/risk/risk_manager.py` 666 вҶ’ 583 Zeilen (-83), neuer Test-File `tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_trade_gate.py` 410 Zeilen, `src/bot/components/risk/__init__.py` +2 Zeilen (TradeGate-Export), `tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_scaffold_imports.py` +2 Zeilen (`TradeGate` im `__all__`-Set erwartet).

### Refactored
- **ARCH-H2 Phase 1 PR-7: Extract `RiskStatePersistence` component (#326)**: DB truth-source I/O (#188) fГјr `DailyStats` wird aus `src/risk/risk_manager.py` in die neue Komponente `src/bot/components/risk/persistence.py` ausgelagert. `RiskStatePersistence` kapselt die drei DB-Pfade (`load_stats` / `save_stats` / `get_historical_stats`) gegen die `risk_stats`-Tabelle und enthГӨlt KEINE Business-Logik вҖ” reines Daten-I/O. `RiskManager` wird dГјnner Delegator: `load_stats_from_db`, `_save_stats_to_db` und `get_historical_stats_from_db` rufen jetzt die Komponente auf; die `_use_db`-Gate und der `get_session`-Patch-Point bleiben am Modul fГјr Test-KompatibilitГӨt erhalten (`_get_session_proxy` Indirection lГӨsst die Phase-0 Characterization-Tests mit `patch("src.risk.risk_manager.get_session", ...)` weiterhin funktionieren). **Contract-preservation (byte-identisch)**: (1) **Computed-Fields-Strip on load** вҖ” die drei `@property`-Felder `net_pnl` / `return_percent` / `win_rate` werden per benannter Konstante `_COMPUTED_DAILYSTATS_FIELDS` aus dem JSON-Blob entfernt BEVOR `DailyStats(**data)` aufgerufen wird (explizit statt inline-Tuple); verifiziert durch `test_strips_all_three_computed_fields` (hard-locks `set(_COMPUTED_DAILYSTATS_FIELDS) == {"net_pnl", "return_percent", "win_rate"}`). (2) **Exception-Swallow-Contract** вҖ” alle drei Code-Pfade (load / save / historical) swallow `Exception`, loggen `logger.warning(...)`, und geben ihren No-Op-Return (`None` / silent / `[]`) zurГјck; der Bot crashed nicht bei transientem DB-Fehler, der in-memory `_daily_stats` bleibt Source-of-Truth, und der nГӨchste erfolgreiche Write resynct die DB. (3) **Upsert-Semantik** вҖ” `save_stats` macht UPDATE auf existing row, INSERT auf miss; `daily_pnl` spiegelt `stats.net_pnl` (not `total_pnl`), `trades_count` = `trades_executed`, `is_halted` = `is_trading_halted`. **Import-Cycle fix**: `RiskStatePersistence` wird lazy in `RiskManager.__init__` importiert (nicht top-level), da `src.bot.components.risk.persistence` Гјber `src.bot.__init__` вҶ’ `BotWorker` вҶ’ `risk_manager` zurГјck zirkuliert. 25 neue Unit-Tests in `tests/unit/bot/components/risk/test_persistence.py` decken ab: Enabled-Gate (disabled-bei-None-config / disabled-bei-None-factory / enabled-wenn-beide-da / Disabled-No-Op auf allen drei Methoden), Load-Path (Row-Hit + Miss + Strip-All-Three-Computed-Fields + Exception-Swallow + JSON-Decode-Error-Swallow), Save-Path (INSERT-new + UPDATE-existing + Round-Trip saveвҶ’load byte-equal + Exception-Swallow + `net_pnl`-serialisation), Historical-Path (parsed rows + empty list + Exception-Swallow), Protocol-Conformance (`isinstance(p, RiskStatePersistenceProtocol)`), DailyStats-Class-Injection (Injection-Hook + Lazy-Fallback), FaГ§ade-Delegation-Surface (load assigns, save delegates, historical delegates, no-op-when-disabled, running-loop vs. no-running-loop scheduling path). Plus 4 Facade-Branch-Coverage-Top-Ups fГјr `get_remaining_trades` per-symbol-before-init, deprecated sync `get_historical_stats`, zero-empty `get_performance_summary`, und `return_percent`-divide-by-zero-Guard. Coverage: `src/risk/risk_manager.py` **86% вҶ’ 87%**, `src/bot/components/risk/persistence.py` **0% вҶ’ 99%** (verbleibende Line 39 ist `if TYPE_CHECKING:`-Block). Alle 50 + 1 Phase-0 Characterization-Tests bleiben grГјn (1 skipped wie vorgesehen). Verbleibende uncovered Lines in `risk_manager.py`: `calculate_position_size` (out-of-scope, Future-PositionSizer-Komponente), `get_performance_summary` non-empty history (Reports-Modul), ImportError-Fallback fГјr sqlalchemy (dead in env).

- **Bot instrumentation: signal emission, trade execution, position monitor tick metrics (PR-3 of #327)**. Call sites added to `src/bot/bot_worker.py::_analyze_symbol_locked` (after `strategy.generate_signal()`, only for long/short вҖ” neutral signals are ignored), `src/bot/components/trade_executor.py::execute` (wraps `place_market_order` with `time.perf_counter()`; result label = `success` when the exchange returns an order, `rejected` on `None`, `failed` on exception вҖ” emitted from a `finally` block so exception paths still land in the counter), and `src/bot/components/position_monitor.py::monitor` (refactored the tick body into `_monitor_body` so the timing wrapper records the full duration even when the body raises). New observability-registry gauges `bot_open_positions{bot_id, exchange}` + `bot_daily_pnl{bot_id, exchange}` are populated by `_collect_observability_bot_gauges` вҖ” a new helper wired into the existing 15 s `collect_bot_metrics` loop that pulls open-position counts from `TradeRecord` (status=`open`) and net PnL from `RiskManager.get_daily_stats().net_pnl`. The old `src/monitoring/metrics.py` legacy registry is NOT touched вҖ” both registries are populated in parallel until a follow-up PR retires the legacy one. `lifespan` in `src/api/main_app.py` also stamps `app_build_commit{commit=<BUILD_COMMIT env, "unknown" if unset>}=1` on startup so Grafana can diff deployments. All emissions are gated by `try/except` (metrics must never break trading) but NOT by the `prometheus_enabled` feature flag: `.inc()` / `.observe()` are atomic and cheaper than the flag read, and the endpoint itself still 404s when the flag is off. Tests: new `tests/unit/observability/test_bot_instrumentation.py` (8 cases) вҖ” signal counter with long labels, neutral signal no-op, trade-executor success (counter + histogram delta), rejected-on-None, failed-on-exception, position-monitor tick histogram, tick histogram still observed when body raises, collector gauges set open-positions from DB + daily PnL from risk manager. All 334 pre-existing tests in `tests/unit/bot/`, `tests/unit/observability/`, `tests/unit/api/middleware/` still pass; new total 342. Risk + Exchange + Alert instrumentation deferred to PR-4. Bilingual `Anleitungen/observability_setup.md` extended with a "Bot Metrics" section (DE + EN) that documents every label's value vocabulary.
- **Risk gate + exchange API metrics instrumentation (PR-4 of #327)**. `RiskManager.can_trade()` in `src/risk/risk_manager.py` now emits `risk_trade_gate_decisions_total` (Counter, labels `bot_id`, `decision`) on every branch: `allow`, `block_max_trades`, `block_daily_loss`, `block_max_trades_symbol`, `block_daily_loss_symbol`, `block_global_halted`, `block_symbol_halted`, `block_uninitialized`. The per-symbol loss limit has two state-mutating sites вҖ” the eager gate-time check in `can_trade` and the lazy write in `record_trade_exit` вҖ” but only the gate-time path is counted, since the exit-time flip changes state without gating any trade; counting both would double-count a single halt. `bot_id` uses `bot_config_id` when available and falls back to `"unknown"` for test harnesses that instantiate a bare `RiskManager`. Exchange adapters: `HTTPExchangeClientMixin._request` (the REST entry point shared by Bitget, Weex, BingX, Bitunix) now emits `exchange_api_requests_total{exchange,endpoint,status}` + `exchange_api_request_duration_seconds{exchange,endpoint}` on every call; `status` is `ok` / `error` / `circuit_open`. `HyperliquidClient._cb_call` gets the same pair with `endpoint` derived from the SDK method name (`market_open`, `user_state`, `cancel` вҖҰ) вҖ” stable and cardinality-safe. New helper `_collapse_endpoint` in `src/exchanges/base.py` folds numeric IDs, hex blobs, UUIDs and query strings inside endpoint paths to `/{id}` as defence in depth against a future adapter embedding an order-id in the URL. WebSocket: `exchange_websocket_connected{exchange}` gauge is set from both the new `ExchangeWebSocketClient` base (`src/exchanges/websockets/base.py`, covering `bitget_ws.py` + `hyperliquid_ws.py`) вҖ” on successful connect, on explicit disconnect, and on the reconnect path in `run_forever` вҖ” and from the legacy `ExchangeWebSocket` subclasses in `src/exchanges/{bitget,bingx,weex,bitunix,hyperliquid}/websocket.py` for parity across the whole adapter surface. Alert emission instrumentation (`risk_alerts_emitted_total`) is **deliberately deferred** вҖ” the alert logic currently lives on `BotWorker` and would collide with the parallel PR-3; it will land together with the AlertThrottler extraction in #326 phase 1. No changes to `src/bot/bot_worker.py`, `src/bot/components/trade_executor.py` or `src/bot/components/position_monitor.py` in this PR. Tests: new `tests/unit/observability/test_risk_instrumentation.py` (10 cases) exercises every `decision` branch including the `unknown`-fallback label and asserts `record_trade_exit` never emits a gate decision. New `tests/unit/observability/test_exchange_instrumentation.py` (9 cases) covers REST success, REST failure, REST without circuit-breaker, endpoint-collapsing for numeric/hex/UUID/query-string inputs, Hyperliquid SDK success + failure paths, and WebSocket gauge transitions (connect вҶ’ 1, disconnect вҶ’ 0, and the drop-handled-in-run_forever path). Bilingual `Anleitungen/observability_setup.md` extended with "Risk-Metrics (PR-4)" and "Exchange-Metrics (PR-4)" sections (DE + EN).
- Grafana dashboards + docker-compose stack for local Prometheus+Grafana setup, full observability setup guide (PR-5 of #327, closes observability instrumentation stream).
- **HTTP metrics middleware with template-path label collapsing: requests, latency, in-flight gauges (PR-2 of #327)**. New module `src/api/middleware/metrics.py` wires the three HTTP metrics from PR-1 (`http_requests_total`, `http_request_duration_seconds`, `http_requests_in_flight`) on every request. Implemented as a pure ASGI middleware (not `BaseHTTPMiddleware`) so the matched-route template can be resolved via `Route.matches(scope)` **before** the downstream app runs вҖ” this is what keeps the in-flight gauge's `inc()` / `dec()` pair aligned on the same label value even in the exception path. Registered **last** in `create_app()` so it is the outermost layer of the middleware stack and its histogram captures the wall-clock cost of every other middleware (auth, rate limit, security headers). Gated end-to-end by `prometheus_enabled`: when the flag is off the middleware is a pure pass-through (no timing, no label allocation, no metric observation). Cardinality hardening: `GET /api/bots/42`, `/api/bots/17`, `/api/bots/999` all collapse onto `path="/api/bots/{bot_id}"` вҖ” the raw request path is never used as a label. Unmatched routes (404 on routes that do not exist) use the sentinel `path="<unmatched>"`. The `/metrics` endpoint itself is NOT instrumented (early-return on `request.url.path.startswith("/metrics")`) to avoid a self-observing loop on every Prometheus scrape. Exception path is fully covered via `try/finally`: a handler raising `RuntimeError` still dec's `http_requests_in_flight` and records a 500 on `http_requests_total`. Tests: new `tests/unit/api/middleware/test_metrics_middleware.py` (6 cases) вҖ” flag off = no observation, flag on happy path, parametrised path collapsing, unmatched path sentinel, exception path (status=500 + in-flight drain), `/metrics` is not self-instrumented. Legacy `src/monitoring/middleware.py` + `src/monitoring/metrics.py` still exist and still register with the prometheus_client default registry вҖ” they are **superseded** by this new middleware (which writes to the dedicated observability `CollectorRegistry` from PR-1) and will be removed in a follow-up PR once no code imports them. Bilingual `Anleitungen/observability_setup.md` extended with an "HTTP metrics" section (DE + EN).
- **Prometheus metrics infrastructure (#327 PR-1)**: flag-gated `/metrics` endpoint behind Basic-Auth, metric definitions in `src/observability/metrics.py` (HTTP / Bot / Risk / Exchange / System groups) backed by a dedicated `CollectorRegistry`, new `PROMETHEUS_ENABLED` feature flag registered in `config/feature_flags.py` + `MonitoringConfig` on `config/settings.py`, new env vars `METRICS_BASIC_AUTH_USER` / `METRICS_BASIC_AUTH_PASSWORD` (documented in `.env.example`). Endpoint contract: flag off вҶ’ 404 (existence not leaked), flag on without/with-wrong credentials вҶ’ 401 with `WWW-Authenticate: Basic`, flag on with correct credentials вҶ’ 200 and Prometheus text exposition body. Credential comparison is timing-safe via `secrets.compare_digest`. No `.inc()` / `.observe()` / `.set()` call sites yet вҖ” those land in PR-2 (HTTP middleware), PR-3 (BotWorker/TradeExecutor/PositionMonitor) and PR-4 (RiskStateManager + ExchangeClient adapters). Grafana dashboards ship in PR-5. New bilingual stub `Anleitungen/observability_setup.md`. Tests: `tests/unit/observability/test_metrics_endpoint.py` covers all four contract points plus the "flag on, no credentials configured" edge case.

### Refactored
- **ARCH-H1 Phase 1 finalize: `BotWorker` ist jetzt pure Composition (#285)**: `BotWorker` erbt nicht mehr von den vier historischen Mixins (`TradeExecutorMixin`, `PositionMonitorMixin`, `TradeCloserMixin`, `NotificationsMixin`) вҖ” die Klassendeklaration ist jetzt schlicht `class BotWorker:` und `BotWorker.__mro__` reduziert sich auf `(BotWorker, object)`. Alle Mixin-Methoden sind als explizite, dГјnne Forwarder an die Komponenten (`self._notifier`, `self._position_monitor`, `self._trade_executor`, `self._trade_closer`) inlined. Abweichung von der Issue-Spec (#285 forderte das LГ¶schen der vier Mixin-Module): die Shim-Module `src/bot/notifications.py`, `src/bot/position_monitor.py`, `src/bot/trade_closer.py`, `src/bot/trade_executor.py` bleiben bestehen, da mehrere Test-Harnesses die Mixin-Klassen direkt importieren (`PositionMonitorMixin`, `TradeExecutorMixin` als Test-Doubles) und `tests/integration/test_manual_close_full_flow.py` Symbole auf dem `src.bot.notifications`-Modulpfad patcht. Die Composition-Invariante (MRO == `(BotWorker, object)`) ist dennoch strikt erfГјllt вҖ” das Ziel des Refactors (keine Mixin-Diamant-Vererbung, keine impliziten `super()`-Hopping) ist erreicht, ohne Test-Kollateral zu erzeugen. 516 unit tests in `tests/unit/bot/`, `tests/unit/services/`, `tests/unit/api/` alle grГјn.

### Security
- **Hyperliquid EIP-712 payload validator + builder-fee bounds (#257, SEC-005 / SEC-008)**: Defense-in-depth gegen geld-bewegende Signaturen. Neues Modul `src/exchanges/hyperliquid/eip712_validator.py` pinnt drei Invarianten vor jedem EIP-712-Signing: (1) **`chain_id`** вҖ” Mainnet 42161 (Arbitrum One) / Testnet 421614 (Arbitrum Sepolia) werden per `assert_chain_id(cid, demo_mode=...)` gegen den erwarteten Netzwerk-Pin geprГјft; verhindert Cross-Chain-Replay einer manipulierten SDK-Signatur. (2) **`primaryType`-Whitelist** вҖ” nur `{Order, Cancel, CancelByCloid, ModifyOrder, BatchModify, UpdateLeverage, UpdateIsolatedMargin, ApproveBuilderFee, ScheduleCancel}` dГјrfen signiert werden; `ApproveAgent` / `Withdraw` / `UsdSend` werden explizit verweigert (zusГӨtzliche Schicht Гјber SafeExchange's Methodenname-Filter). (3) **Builder-Fee-Bounds** вҖ” `MIN/MAX_BUILDER_FEE_TENTHS_BPS = 1 / 100` (0.001% вҖ“ 0.1%) als Konstanten, Assertion in `HyperliquidClient.approve_builder_fee` checked sowohl die Integer-Form (`assert_builder_fee_tenths_bps`) als auch den auf den Draht gehenden Prozent-String (`assert_builder_fee_pct`). Regression-Guard gegen den 10x-zu-hoch-Vorfall (2026-03-17): `builder_fee=1000` wird abgelehnt, SDK wird nicht aufgerufen. Client-Konstruktion speichert `self._expected_chain_id` und nutzt die MIN/MAX-Konstanten statt hartcodierter `1 <= fee <= 100`. 29 neue Unit-Tests in `tests/unit/exchanges/test_hyperliquid_eip712_validator.py` decken Happy-Path Mainnet/Testnet, Chain-Mismatch (testnet-Chain in Mainnet-Modus und umgekehrt), primaryType-Whitelist-VerstГ¶Гҹe, Wire-Format-Parsing (`0.01%`, `0.01`, Whitespace, `abc` / `-0.01%` / scientific-notation rejected), Builder-Fee-Out-of-Range, Non-Int/Bool-Reject und einen dedizierten `test_rejects_10x_regression` ab; plus 1 neuer Test `test_approve_rejects_fee_beyond_cap` in `test_hyperliquid_builder.py`, der den End-to-End-Call `HyperliquidClient.approve_builder_fee()` mit `fee=1000` gegen den Validator fГјhrt und asserted dass das SDK nicht gerufen wird.
### Tests
- **ARCH-C1 Phase 0: Characterization-Tests fГјr `src/api/routers/trades.py` (#325)**: Neue Datei `tests/unit/api/test_trades_router_characterization.py` mit 61 Tests, die das aktuelle observable Verhalten der vier noch nicht extrahierten Trades-Endpoints einfrieren (`POST /api/trades/sync`, `GET /api/trades/{trade_id}`, `GET /api/trades/{trade_id}/risk-state`, `PUT /api/trades/{trade_id}/tp-sl`). Dient als Safety-Net vor den Extract-PRs PR-1/2/3 von #325. Deckt u. a. ab: Auth-401 pro Endpoint, 404-Fusion (nicht-vorhanden + nicht-eigener User indistinguishable), 422-Schema-Validation (`extra='forbid'`, callback_pct-Range), TP/SL-Mutex auf beiden Flag-Pfaden (legacy=400, manager=422), side-/entry-abhГӨngige 400er, Response-Shape-Divergenz zwischen Legacy (`{"status": "ok", ...}`) und Manager (`TpSlResponse`), RSM-`classify_close`-Dispatch in `sync_trades` inkl. - **ARCH-H1 Phase 0 PR-2: Characterization-Tests fГјr `BotWorker.graceful_stop()` (#270)**: Neuer Test-Modul `tests/unit/bot/test_bot_worker_graceful_stop.py` friert das aktuelle, observable Verhalten von `graceful_stop` ein, bevor in spГӨteren PRs Mixin-Extraktion beginnt. 11 Tests decken alle Top-Level-Branches ab: `_shutting_down` Flag wird gesetzt, `self.stop()` Delegation ist unbedingt, Happy-Path mit idle `_operation_in_progress`-Event, Timeout-Path wenn das Event cleared bleibt, DB-Query gibt das dokumentierte 7-Key-Dict zurГјck (`symbol`/`side`/`size`/`entry_price`/`demo_mode`/`has_tp`/`has_sl`), Leere-Trades-Liste вҶ’ `[]`, Exception im DB-Query wird swallowed + `stop()` lГӨuft trotzdem, Exception in `client.get_open_positions()` swallowed + DB-Positionen werden weiterhin zurГјckgegeben, Demo + Live-Clients werden beide gepollt wenn gesetzt, `None`-Clients werden Гјbersprungen, Status-Transition zu `STOPPED` lГӨuft Гјber die `stop()`-Delegation. Coverage von `src/bot/bot_worker.py` geht damit von **78% вҶ’ 84%**, `graceful_stop` selbst (Zeilen 523-600) von ~0% auf вүҘ95% вҖ” nur noch der kommentierte `pass # TP/SL are protective вҖ” leave them in place` no-op-Branch in Zeile 569 ist ungedeckt. Entspricht dem 85%-Gate-Schritt aus `Anleitungen/refactor_plan_bot_worker_composition.md`; die letzte Prozentpunkt-LГјcke schlieГҹt Phase-0-PR-3 (`_analyze_and_trade*` + `_analyze_symbol*`).
- **ARCH-H1 Phase 0 PR-3: Characterization-Tests fГјr `_send_daily_summary` + self-managed-Strategie-Dispatch (#272)**: Neuer Test-Modul `tests/unit/bot/test_bot_worker_daily_summary.py` mit 10 fokussierten Tests, die zusГӨtzlich zum PR#271-Fundament die restlichen `BotWorker`-LГјcken schlieГҹen, die das 85%-Coverage-Gate aus `Anleitungen/refactor_plan_bot_worker_composition.md` blockieren.
